## 1. [The 13th Annual Young Comedians Special (1989)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-1989?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-1989&utm_term=the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-1989)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-1989?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-1989&amp;utm_term=the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-1989"><img alt="the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-tt0295050-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-13th-annual-young-comedians-special-tt0295050-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"The 13th Annual Young Comedians Special" (1989) is a must-see for comedy enthusiasts, featuring a live audience and some of the most promising stand-up comedians of that era. Hosted by the talented Jann Karam, this TV special presents a showcase of up-and-coming comedic talents including Drake Sather and Rob Schneider. With a runtime of 1 hour, the show is directed by Ellen Brown and written by Warren Thomas. Produced by Brillstein-Grey Productions, the event was held in the United States and delivered in English. This special has earned an IMDb rating of 6.3 from 60 votes, showcasing its appeal among comedy fans. The Young Comedians Special offers a blend of raw talent and fresh humor, making it an enjoyable experience for viewers of all ages. While the show aired in 1989, its timeless appeal continues to be appreciated. If you are a fan of stand-up comedy, this event is a must-watch. Enjoy the unforgettable performances of Jann Karam, Drake Sather, and Rob Schneider in "The 13th Annual Young Comedians Special"! 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy
- Rated: TV-MA
- Runtime: 1h
- Directed by: Ellen Brown
- Starring: Jann Karam, Drake Sather, Rob Schneider
- Box Office:

## 2. [Martians Go Home (1989)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/martians-go-home-1989?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=martians-go-home-1989&utm_term=martians-go-home-1989)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/martians-go-home-1989?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=martians-go-home-1989&amp;utm_term=martians-go-home-1989"><img alt="martians-go-home-tt0100116-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/martians-go-home-tt0100116-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Martians Go Home" is a hilarious sci-fi comedy that follows the misadventures of songwriter Mark Devereaux. One unfortunate mistake leads to a full-scale invasion of wise-cracking green Martians, determined to disrupt life on Earth. Despite their lack of danger, these unwelcome guests quickly become the most irritating, distracting presence on the planet. Caught in the crossfire, Mark must uncover the secret behind their arrival and find a way to send them back to Mars before they drive everyone completely bonkers! With a star-studded cast, including Randy Quaid, Margaret Colin, and Anita Morris, this 1989 cult classic will have you laughing from start to finish. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Sci-Fi
- Rated: PG-13
- Runtime: 1h 29min
- Directed by: David Odell
- Starring: Randy Quaid, Margaret Colin, Anita Morris

## 3. [Necessary Roughness (1991)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/necessary-roughness-1991?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=necessary-roughness-1991&utm_term=necessary-roughness-1991)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/necessary-roughness-1991?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=necessary-roughness-1991&amp;utm_term=necessary-roughness-1991"><img alt="necessary-roughness-tt0102517-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/necessary-roughness-tt0102517-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Necessary Roughness" is a 1991 sports comedy film directed by Stan Dragoti, starring Scott Bakula, Hector Elizondo, and Robert Loggia. The movie follows the story of Texas State University Fightin' Armadillos as they form a football team from their actual student body due to NCAA sanctions. Without any scholarships, these underdogs must navigate through various challenges, including a bar fight, the wrath of a strict college dean, and the pressure to perform in the face of adversity. Amidst all, they discover camaraderie, team spirit, and the essence of true sportsmanship. With a runtime of 1h 48min and a PG-13 content rating, "Necessary Roughness" is a fun-filled ride filled with humor, heart, and some unforgettable performances. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Sport
- Rated: PG-13
- Runtime: 1h 48min
- Directed by: Stan Dragoti
- Starring: Scott Bakula, Hector Elizondo, Robert Loggia
- Box Office:
 - Budget: $13,500,000 (estimated)
 - Gross USA: $26,255,594

## 4. [The 43rd Annual Primetime Emmy Awards (1991)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-43rd-annual-primetime-emmy-awards-1991?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-43rd-annual-primetime-emmy-awards-1991&utm_term=the-43rd-annual-primetime-emmy-awards-1991)

"The 43rd Annual Primetime Emmy Awards" is a captivating television special from 1991, celebrating the outstanding achievements in the world of primetime television. This awards show takes you on a riveting journey through the memorable performances and unforgettable moments of that year, including the most outstanding actors, actresses, and programs. Academy of Television Arts and Sciences (ATAS) brings together a star-studded lineup of presenters and honorees, including Debbie Allen, Kirstie Alley, and Loni Anderson. The esteemed Bruce Eric Kaplan, Herbert Sargent, and Andrew Smith collaborate as writers under the expert direction of Walter C. Miller. "The 43rd Annual Primetime Emmy Awards" delivers an engaging blend of glamour and inspiration, as it showcases the phenomenal talents that make the world of television so enchanting. This special captures the essence of the Emmy Awards' grand tradition of celebrating the best in the industry, leaving viewers with a memorable experience. Don't miss this captivating glimpse into the illustrious world of primetime television - tune in for "The 43rd Annual Primetime Emmy Awards. "

## 5. [Home Alone 2: Lost in New York (1992)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-1992?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-1992&utm_term=home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-1992)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-1992?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-1992&amp;utm_term=home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-1992"><img alt="home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-tt0104431-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/home-alone-2-lost-in-new-york-tt0104431-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Home Alone 2: Lost in New York" is a delightful holiday adventure that continues the iconic tale of young Kevin McCallister. A year after defending his home from two bumbling burglars, Kevin finds himself embarking on another perilous journey in the bustling city of New York. Stranded on his way to Florida, he crosses paths with the notorious duo who have set their sights on robbing a prominent toy store. Filled with amusing mishaps, outrageous set-ups and a touch of Christmas cheer, this sequel will have you laughing and feeling warm-hearted all the way through. Directed by Chris Columbus and starring Macaulay Culkin, Joe Pesci and Daniel Stern, the film is a perfect blend of adventure, comedy, and crime. Get ready to join Kevin as he navigates the busy streets of New York City, encountering a series of memorable characters along the way. Will he manage to outsmart the bad guys once again? This family-friendly classic is a must-watch during the holiday season and offers plenty of laughs for everyone. 



<br>

## 7. [Demolition Man (1993)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/demolition-man-1993?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=demolition-man-1993&utm_term=demolition-man-1993)

<br>

Demolition Man, a high-energy action-thriller from 1993, follows the story of a grizzled police officer, played by Sylvester Stallone, who is brought out of suspended animation to face off against his old nemesis, portrayed by Wesley Snipes. Unleashed in a future society that is the antithesis of violence, Stallone's character must navigate a world where peace is enforced, censorship is omnipresent, and the most thrilling encounter is visiting a museum display. This edge-of-your-seat, cyberpunk adventure, directed by Marco Brambilla and co-starring Sandra Bullock, masterfully intertwines action and sci-fi themes, keeping viewers at the edge of their seats with its intricate storyline. A critical success, Demolition Man received 1 win and 7 nominations, making it a must-watch for fans of the genre. 



<br>

## 8. [The Beverly Hillbillies (1993)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-beverly-hillbillies-1993?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-beverly-hillbillies-1993&utm_term=the-beverly-hillbillies-1993)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-beverly-hillbillies-1993?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-beverly-hillbillies-1993&amp;utm_term=the-beverly-hillbillies-1993"><img alt="the-beverly-hillbillies-tt0106400-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-beverly-hillbillies-tt0106400-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"The Beverly Hillbillies" is a comedy-family film from 1993, directed by Penelope Spheeris. The story follows Jed Clampett, a kind-hearted redneck, who strikes it rich when he discovers black oil on his land. Along with his family, he moves to the ritzy Beverly Hills. The film offers a satirical take on the "rags to riches" trope, exploring the cultural clash between the down-to-earth Clampetts and their sophisticated new surroundings. The ensemble cast, including Diedrich Bader, Erika Eleniak, and Jim Varney, delivers a delightful blend of humour and heart. "The Beverly Hillbillies" provides an entertaining exploration of the "fish out of water" concept, while maintaining a family-friendly appeal. Widely recognized for its comedic elements and relatable rags-to-riches narrative, this classic film is sure to resonate with audiences. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Family
- Rated: PG
- Runtime: 1h 32min
- Directed by: Penelope Spheeris
- Starring: Diedrich Bader, Erika Eleniak, Jim Varney
- Box Office:
 - Budget: $25,000,000 (estimated)
 - Gross USA: $44,029,386
 - Opening Weekend USA: $9,525,375

"Buddy" is an animated short film from 1993 that provides a visual representation of the popular Adam Sandler audio skit. The story unfolds on a train, where two buddies, two dudes, and two homies engage in entertaining interactions and banter. The film combines vibrant animations with witty dialogues, offering a unique blend of humor and creativity. It features voice performances from accomplished comedians like Tim Herlihy, Tim Meadows, and Rob Schneider. Produced by Warner Bros. Records, "Buddy" is a captivating short film that appeals to fans of animation and comedy. The film is in English and holds an IMDb rating of 5.6.

Starring Jean-Claude Van Damme, Rob Schneider, and Lela Rochon, "Knock Off" boasts a gripping plot filled with twists and turns and non-stop action. The film was produced by Knock Films A. V. V. , MDP Worldwide, and Film Workshop, with Hark Tsui and Steven E. de Souza as director and writer respectively. "Knock Off" was released on 1998-09-04 and has since garnered an IMDb rating of 4.8, with a box office result of $10,319,915 on an estimated budget of $30,000,000. The film has notable similarities with movies such as "The Order, " "Special Forces, " and "City Central, " among others. With its engaging plot, star-studded cast, and high-stakes action, "Knock Off" promises an unforgettable cinematic experience. It's definitely a must-watch for fans of high school comedies and those who enjoy a dose of dark humor. "Leo" is a heartwarming animated family comedy set to release in 2023. This engaging tale follows the adventurous journey of a 74-year-old lizard named Leo and his wise turtle friend, who decide to escape from the terrarium of a Florida elementary school classroom where they have lived for decades. As these charming characters embark on their daring adventure through the Everglades of Florida, audiences of all ages will be captivated by their colorful escapades and heartfelt experiences. "Leo" is meticulously crafted by a talented trio of directors, Robert Marianetti, Robert Smigel, and David Wachtenheim, and brought to life by the whimsical screenplay of Robert Smigel, Adam Sandler, and Paul Sado. Sandler also stars alongside Bill Burr and Cecily Strong in this delightful film. The movie is a collaborative effort between Netflix, Animal Logic, and Happy Madison Productions, with production taking place in the USA and Australia. Filled with laughter, heart, and a touch of adventure, "Leo" promises to be a memorable watching experience for the whole family. With a runtime of 1h 42min, this feel-good animated comedy is perfect for a cozy movie night or a celebration with friends. Mark your calendars for its release on November 21, 2023, and don't forget to share your enthusiasm with everyone eagerly awaiting its premiere.
